Naval Conference Unlikely to Succeed; Britain and the United States Prepare for Military Expansion; Tripartite Talks Face Wide Disagreement; British Cabinet Decides to Increase Military Spending 48

(London) The Morning Post reports that the British Cabinet has now made a concrete decision on the policy of expanding armaments. An important statement on this matter will be issued soon. (National Telegram on the 27th)

(London) As hopes for the 1935 Naval Conference gradually diminish, the British Cabinet held a meeting this morning at 11:00 AM. It is reported that a major decision has been made to increase spending on the navy and air force. According to reliable sources, the Cabinet has also approved an increase in the army budget. Britain will implement a large-scale plan to expand its armaments in the middle of next week, as the government will then submit supplementary funding requests for the army, navy, and air force to Parliament. The preliminary naval talks recently held here have revealed a deep divergence of views among the United States, Britain, and Japan, making the success of next year's naval conference very doubtful. (National Telegram on the 27th)

(London) The Conservative Party's Morning Post reports that the British government has decided to adopt a policy of rearmament. This decision will be announced soon. It is said that the British government has decided to reorganize British defense in the short term. In addition to the existing plans to strengthen the air force, it also intends to strengthen the navy. The hope of reaching an agreement on the formation of navies among various countries is gradually fading, so the need for Britain to expand its navy is becoming increasingly urgent. The British government has decided to expand its navy, and the scope of expansion, which will be considered in the current talks between British and American representatives, will be above and beyond what is currently being considered, pending the failure of naval negotiations or the indefinite postponement of the naval conference. According to reports, the scope of the British navy's request for expansion includes four items: (1) Building a new battleship fleet; (2) Building 30 new cruisers, bringing the total to 70; (3) Building many destroyers; (4) Building many aircraft carriers. (Havas Telegram on the 27th)

(Washington) The Star newspaper here has learned from well-informed sources that if the next naval conference cannot achieve satisfactory results, the United States plans to start building a new battleship at the beginning of 1936 to replace old ships that have reached their age limit. The last battleship built by the United States was the "West Virginia," which was launched and commissioned in 1921. (Havas Telegram on the 26th)

(London) Britain Does Not Intend to Use Goods to Repay American War Debts: It is reported that the British government's reply to the United States does not approve of the United States re-raising the war debt issue. The reply will be delivered to US Secretary of State Hull by Ambassador Lindsay to the United States on Wednesday and will be released on Thursday. The wording is very mild, but it firmly opposes the US proposal to repay the debt with goods. It is heard that the British reply used conciliatory language because Britain wants to ease the current tense atmosphere between Britain and the United States caused by the naval preparatory conference. (National Telegram on the 26th)

British and American Experts Reopen Meeting 49

(London) Privy Councilor Baldwin said in the House of Commons today regarding the naval talks in progress that the location of the 1935 Naval Conference has not yet been decided. Japan has not yet made a demand for naval equality. As for the progress of the talks, matters are confidential and he cannot elaborate. (Reuters Telegram on the 27th)

(London) During the meeting of British and American naval experts on the 21st of this month, the British representatives submitted a list of the minimum warships and armaments required for British defense to the American representatives. The American representatives sent this document to Washington to await instructions before holding another meeting. It is now learned that the British and American representatives or experts are scheduled to reopen the meeting tomorrow. The demands made by Britain have been studied by the Washington Naval Department. It is heard that the department believes that Britain only knows how to make demands without considering whether the other party can agree, and has not considered the revision of the London Naval Treaty. Therefore, the US government has instructed the US representatives that if a compromise can be reached on the 1935 Naval Conference, the British government should explain its demands in detail and propose procedures for conducting the naval conference. As for the current negotiations, if they fail, Washington believes that there is no need to express an opinion on the demands made by Britain. It seems that the American representatives will still maintain a wait-and-see attitude, waiting for Britain to explain its views in detail, and will not make any suggestions, which can be inferred. (Havas Telegram on the 26th)

Japan Discusses Countermeasures; Seeks to Break Through the Current Ratio; Naval Department Increases Personnel to Britain 50

(Tokyo) Observing the situation of the London disarmament preparatory consultation, Britain and the United States seem not yet to have decided on any specific matters regarding the disarmament conference. The real policy decision will be made around October. After yesterday's cabinet meeting, Foreign Minister Hirota and Navy Minister Osumi stayed behind to exchange information on individual talks and discuss the fundamental policy on disarmament. As a result, both sides agreed to reject all existing treaty-defined quantitative plans based on current strengths and unanimously advocated that Japan propose a concrete plan to the disarmament conference to reduce both quality and quantity at the same time. Not only should countries with high levels of armaments reduce their holdings, but countries with inferior armaments should also reduce their strengths, thereby contributing to the world's disarmament efforts. The outline of this counter-proposal can be drafted in October this year after Ambassador Saito to the United States and Ambassador Sato to France return home. Moreover, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that, given the current situation in Europe, even if France and Italy cannot participate, it is still highly desirable to achieve a disarmament agreement among Britain, the United States, and Japan (Dentsu Telegram on the 27th) (Tokyo) In view of the progress of the British-American naval preparatory negotiations, the Japanese Navy Ministry has decided to send another military officer who is well-versed in naval affairs to Britain to assist Ambassador Matsudaira. The Naval General Staff ordered Colonel Masasuke Shimomura to proceed to Britain on the 28th aboard the Tatsuta Maru (Nichi-Rengo Telegram on the 27th)

Italian Newspaper Argues that Russia Should Participate 51

Rome: The "Fascist Lavoro" newspaper claims that the Soviet Union and Germany must be invited to participate in the 1935 Naval Conference, and especially insists on inviting the Soviet Union to be appropriate. The newspaper claims that "The Soviet Union is a power in the Pacific, Baltic, and Black Sea regions. The main defect of the Washington Treaty is that the Soviet Union did not join. Simple common sense shows us that a naval conference without the Soviet Union will have a serious defect." (TASS Telegram on the 26th)

Prospects for Next Year's Naval Conference: Britain Builds Ships Beyond the Scope of the Treaty; Liberal Party Newspaper Considers Government Unwise 52

(London) The Liberal Party's organ, the "Manchester Guardian," published an editorial this morning discussing the prospects for the 1935 Naval Conference and commenting on the current naval preparatory negotiations. It severely criticized the British government's policy, stating that when other countries demanded that our country limit large warships in the past, the government stated that the limit was 56 ships. When the issue of limiting naval armaments was raised for discussion, the general public then realized that the limit for large warships had to be increased from 56 to 70. It is generally believed that the naval construction program drafted by the British Admiralty contains a number of cruisers and destroyers that exceed the limits stipulated by the London Treaty, and the amount exceeded is very large. If the government's intention is indeed like this, then our country has failed to lead the way and is unwise. The main purpose of our country's naval policy should be to extend and strengthen the effectiveness of the Washington and London Naval Treaties. Although the Washington and London Naval Treaties are not perfect, the restrictions on the size and number of warships and the total tonnage of cruisers and destroyers are of great benefit. Therefore, this kind of step can prevent naval armaments competition. If the Washington and London Naval Treaties cannot be extended and remain effective, then armaments competition will inevitably restart. (Havas Telegram on the 27th)

British Government's Plan to Support the Shipping Industry: Adding New Ships to Replace Old Ships 53

(London) According to this morning's newspaper reports, the government will announce its plan to support the British shipping industry in the House of Commons on July 7th. Newspapers expect that the government's method of supporting the shipping industry will be nothing more than providing loan facilities to allow the shipping industry to build new ships in accordance with the ratio of demolishing three old ships and building one new ship. US Navy and Marine Corps Air Squadrons Conduct Long-Distance Flight Exercises Separately 55

(Washington) The Navy Department announced today that while the Army Department's military aircraft are flying from Washington to Alaska, 12 Navy aircraft will also fly from the coast of San Diego to Dutch Harbor, making a long-distance flight of 7,700 miles. The flight is scheduled to depart from the San Diego Naval Base on July 17. The section from Seattle to Anchorage will require a 700-mile non-stop flight. The Army's flight plan is intended to demonstrate the capabilities of Army aviation personnel, while the Navy's flight plan is a continuation of last year's formation flight exercises. On January 11 of this year, six Navy aircraft practiced formation flying, covering a distance of 2,000 miles from San Francisco to Honolulu in one go. Last year, a Navy air squadron also flew directly from the East Coast to Panama. (Guomin News Agency Telegram on the 26th)

This Year's Drought Presents a Global Phenomenon; Caused by Sunspots 65

The World News Agency reported that this year's insufficient rainfall and reduced harvests are a common global phenomenon. The United States and Canada anticipate a record-breaking reduction in wheat harvests due to the drought. Europe has also experienced reduced sugar harvests due to the drought. According to the results of research by Dr. Abbott of the Smithsonian Institution in the United States, the cause of this global phenomenon is that sunspots directly affect the Earth's atmosphere. Currently, sunspots are vast, ranging from 500 to 5,000 miles in diameter, and these sunspots are caused by a major storm condition that cannot be associated with the Earth's climate. Dr. Fujiwara, a technician at the Japan Central Meteorological Observatory, also made the following announcement regarding the current drought situation: "Looking at past statistics, the three years before and after the maximum and minimum periods of sunspots are always warning years for climate change. Last year was the minimum period of sunspots, so there is a common global phenomenon of insufficient rainfall, and temperatures are also higher than usual. This year is the year after the minimum period, so it is still within the warning period for changes."

Representative Dies, a member of the House Currency Committee, stated today that the Treasury Department has already purchased approximately 70 million ounces of silver, but the exact number cannot be determined because the United States is purchasing silver in markets around the world, and the forms issued by the Treasury Department have not yet recorded the recent purchases. According to other sources, the price paid by the United States for silver was previously 44 cents per ounce. Dies also said that the printing bureau is unable to keep up with the printing of new silver certificates issued based on silver. It is estimated that the Treasury Department must purchase 125.4 million ounces to meet the needs of the new bill, that is, 25 percent of silver as currency reserve. Adding the above figure to what the government already has will give the United States a total of approximately 200 million ounces of silver. Treasury officials estimated that the cost of purchasing 125.4 million ounces at a price of 75 cents per ounce would be 94,050,000 yuan, and said that it would be fortunate if the United States could purchase about one-fifth of the world's silver at an average price not exceeding 75 cents. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Record of Japanese Military Appointments (Part 1): Predictions of Future Leaders 84

This month, the Nagoya Shimbun in Japan published a lengthy article titled "The Next Minister of the Military." The article comprehensively examined important figures in the national army and navy, providing detailed evaluations. This is of considerable value as a reference for those in our country who are concerned about the Japanese military, and is specially translated below:

Although it is difficult to predict the lifespan of the Saito Cabinet, it has recently experienced subtle decline and is beset by crises. It is expected that changes will occur soon. The succeeding cabinet is likely to emerge from one of three possibilities: Saito's resurgence, Ugaki's formation, or Kiyoura's formation. As for a Suzuki or Hirata Cabinet, there is virtually no hope.

The so-called dangerous period of 1936 is imminent. Who will be the future army and navy ministers is a major question currently. If the mandate to form a cabinet descends upon Saito again, it is feared that all cabinet members will not change and the current military ministers will not need to be replaced. Otherwise, if Saito retires, a problem arises. We should first seek candidates from the generals, including: 1) Commander of the Kwantung Army, General Hishikari Takashi. However, due to his current position, Hishikari will definitely not transfer to become Army Minister. Moreover, in reality, he is not a military politician, but merely a military commander. 2) Military Councillor General Minami Jiro. General Minami served as Army Minister during the second Wakatsuki Cabinet. Internal criticism was not bad. However, due to his age and lack of decisiveness, he is unlikely to rise to power again. 3) Military Councillor General Watanabe Jotaro. He and Army Minister Hayashi are classmates. He is one of the leading war history researchers in the military and also a reader. Most of his salary is used at Maruzen Bookstore, which shows that he is a scholar. However, he has no experience in military administration, only serving as a troop commander and rich in war experience. 4) Director of Technical Affairs, Ogata Katsuichi. He has the golden kite medal for war merits, but he is only a technical officer and not suitable for the position of Army Minister. Besides the above, among the generals, there are also Honjo Shigeru. Honjo is currently the Chief Aide-de-Camp and not qualified to serve as Army Minister. In addition, the only other candidates for Army Minister are Masaki, Abe, Araki, Matsui, and Kawashima. When Araki became Army Minister, his reputation was very good, but during his two-year tenure, his status declined significantly. Because he is talkative, he is disliked by those who are intentional. He claimed to be sick for some reason, but he was not sick at all and left the post of Army Minister. It is feared that it will not be easy to sit in the chair of the Army Minister again. The most likely of the other four is Army Minister Masaki Jinzaburo of the Kiyoura Cabinet and Army Minister Abe Nobuyuki of the Ugaki Cabinet. Masaki Jinzaburo can match Araki in this extraordinary period. After being transferred from the 8th Division Commander to the 1st Division Commander, he was transferred to Taiwan during the Ugaki Army Minister's time as Commander. During the Manchurian Incident, Chief of Staff Prince Kan'in telegraphed and requested that he serve as Vice Minister. He then went to Beijing and was very compatible with Army Minister Araki. He was credited with guiding various operations in Manchuria and Shanghai for one and a half years and was promoted to General, serving as a Military Councillor. Then, Araki resigned, replaced Hayashi as Inspector General of Education. He is inclusive and has great ambitions and is known for speaking his mind in the parliament. Therefore, within his department, there are calls for him to become Army Minister. However, he can command the three armies but cannot be regarded as a military politician. As for Military Councillor Abe Nobuyuki, he is a giant star in the Ugaki line. During the Hamaguchi Cabinet, he served as Ugaki's Deputy Minister. In June of the fifth year of Showa, he made every effort to break the iron wall of the Minister of Military Affairs' exclusive appointment system and acted as Minister of the Army on behalf of Ugaki. Therefore, he definitely has the experience of being an Army Minister. In principle, he should have served as a minister before Araki. Unexpectedly, the internal situation was complicated. It happened to be the time of the Ugaki line handover and he was changed to the commander of the 4th Division and then the commander of the Taiwan Army. He was only promoted to General in June of last year. In August, according to the regular movement of the army, he was appointed as a military councillor. Although he does not have a golden kite medal, he can definitely be called the only general. However, in today's situation, he may not be in the forefront of becoming a true military politician. If Ugaki forms a cabinet, then he is naturally in his bag. Who is the leader of the next cabinet? According to the general trend, Hayashi Senjuro is still in his original position. According to the constitutional aspect, if the cabinet changes, the cabinet members will naturally resign. However, the precedent of retaining the military ministers, such as the Tanaka Cabinet established in April of the second year of Showa, has been broken. Moreover, according to the current situation, it is feared that Hayashi Senjuro will be difficult to remove from the military. He is rare in the military as a virtuous and respected figure who can maintain military control. There are very few talents who can compare with him. The fact that his brother, Shirakami's problem, caused his resignation to fail was not his true intention. He had to stay in office due to the coercion of the military. From this, it can be seen that the next Army Minister will still belong to Hayashi.

Hebei, Shandong, and Henan: Water Control Projects in Three Provinces Planned by the Yellow River Disaster and Yellow River Benefit Associations, All to Be Completed Before the Great Flood: Kong Xiangrong to Visit Chahar and Suiyuan 86

Beiping Communication: The Yellow River dike project in Hebei, Shandong, and Henan is of great importance. Your reporter today (26th) ordered Kong Xiangrong, a member of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee and director of the labor relief group, to talk about Minister Kong's (Xiangxi) visit to the north this time. Due to time constraints, he did not have time to visit Chahar and Suiyuan, so he specially sent me as a representative to go. I am scheduled to take the Pingbao train north at 4 pm today, first to Zhangjiakou, and then to Suiyuan. The work of blocking the mouth of the Yellow River can be divided into three provinces: Hebei, Henan, and Shandong. 1) Hebei Province: Entrusted by Chairman Yu (Xuezhong) of Hebei Province, from the breach in Shitouzhuang, Changyuan County to Dacheji, a total of more than 30 miles, the dikes are all raised and thickened, exceeding the flood level of the previous year by an average of more than two meters, and the dike is more than eight feet thick. Part of this expenditure is saved from the Yellow River blockage project, and another part is 700,000 yuan, which Hebei will raise in advance. The fundraising methods are: 1. The Hebei Provincial Government negotiated with Minister Kong and agreed to extend the additional donation of Changlu salt for two years through the resolution of the Central Executive Yuan, as a guarantee, and borrowed 500,000 yuan from the Central, China, Communications, and other five banks. 2. The Hebei Provincial Department of Finance raised 200,000 yuan from the Hebei Provincial Bank, which was allocated to the Hebei Yellow River dike raising and thickening expenditure. The Hebei Provincial Government appointed Provincial Committee Member Hu Yuanhui as the Director of the Hebei Yellow River Rehabilitation Project Office, and I was also appointed by the Yellow River Conservancy Commission as the Supervisory Commissioner of the province, and ordered me to send engineers to take turns to supervise, and all the north and south dikes of the Yellow River in Hebei Province will be raised and thickened, so that they will be completed before the great flood. 2) Henan Province: The Henan Yellow River Blockage Project Office was established in October last year. In mid-January this year, I was ordered to serve concurrently. As a result of efforts, the closure project was completed within a month. The Yellow River disaster expenditure in Henan Province was sponsored by Minister Kong, and the original salt tax surcharge guarantee in Henan Province was used to borrow 2 million yuan from the Central Bank. In the future, the project will be the responsibility of the Henan River Affairs Bureau, and members of the Yellow River Disaster and Yellow River Benefit committees will be sent to supervise. At present, all important projects have been started, and it is expected that all dangerous projects will be completed before the great flood. 3) Shandong Province: Agreement has been reached with Chairman Han to have Shandong Province handle all urgent rehabilitation matters on its own. The project plans are all guided by members of the Yellow River Disaster and Yellow River Benefit committees and handled by the Shandong River Affairs Bureau.

Regarding the emergency rehabilitation projects in Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces, the Yellow River Benefit Committee had prepared an estimated plan, which was submitted to the Executive Yuan and sent to the Yellow River Disaster Committee for review and overall planning. The committee then sent the director of the engineering group, Kong Xiangrong, to the three provinces by telegram, and all of them have been included in this rehabilitation project. The Shandong River Affairs Bureau replied that in addition to the estimated dangerous projects, there are also many projects to prepare for water defense. In this way, the water control projects in the three provinces have all been settled. (26th)

Inspection Notes in the Northwest: Special Correspondent of This Newspaper 87

— Geng Ya

Joyfully Looking at Helan Mountain from a Distance

On the 5th, it was raining and not sunny, so we stayed in the same place. All the fellow travelers sat in boredom all day long, with nothing to enjoy. Some told jokes, some drank alcohol and played drinking games, some mended clothes, the camel drivers sang tunes and combed their hair, or twisted the picked camel hair (the weather is getting warmer, the camel hair is gradually falling off, and when it is completely shed in the hot summer, it cannot be transported and must be released) into ropes, each according to his own preferences, in an endless variety. The reporter could not stand the smoke and noise, so he put on a hat and went out to collect wild onions for recreation. Two Mongolians with red tassels, neck hats, hoof sleeves, and long robes galloped from the southwest. They were expected to be officials of the Wangfu. They wanted to say hello to them on the road. They could speak Chinese and said, "They are the Si Ye of the Etok Banner Yamen. Knowing that I came from the southeast, they immediately dismounted and talked to me, and immediately said, "Five ethnic groups are united, we are all one family." Then they asked with great concern, "The three eastern provinces have been captured by the little Japanese. Can the central government get them back?" "Is the Feng Army still in Beijing?" "Are you (referring to the reporter) public lords getting along well?" "The Xuantong Emperor is the nephew of the Japanese. I heard that "he listens to his uncle and is marrying a Japanese woman." Is it true? After the reporter gave a brief answer, he briefly inquired about the Wangfu's management of the people. According to the talk, the prince is passed down from one generation to the next and has four "Jia Langs" (like county chiefs) under his jurisdiction. Each Jia Lang manages five or six "Su Mu Zhang Ges." Each Su Mu Zhang Ge manages a number of yurts and a number of people. The property (cattle and sheep) situation and where they live are all recorded in books for easy collection of food and grass. People who commit crimes are severely punished for theft. Stealing sheep is already a light corporal punishment. Stealing horses often leads to death due to severe punishment. Moreover, it is easy to find traces of livestock stolen in the sandy land, and lamas can also predict where the thieves have gone. It is extremely easy to solve the case, so no one dares to commit crimes. In addition, people mostly live a nomadic life and have little contact with each other, so disputes are reduced. The "every hundred catches two, every fifty catches one" reward sheep collected are based on the amount of property. The yurt money of two or three yuan is collected (the lonely, old, and poor are exempt. The Wangfu also finds ways to support the only son and daughter), which is within the power of the people and will not lead to arrears and punishment. Therefore, the yamen is almost empty and the officials are like eating white salaries. The Wangfu is the private residence of the old prince and the young prince. The yamen is the place for office work. Officials are set up to manage. All major and minor official matters must go through the yamen before being forwarded to the Wangfu. Officials and people who visit the prince, receive distinguished guests, and perform the ritual of kneeling and bowing are the same as in the Qing Dynasty. The doors, windows, courtyards, flower gardens, and screens of the Wangfu Yamen are all in the Chinese style, but the spring couplets posted on the doorposts are not in Chinese but in Mongolian. The young prince can already lead troops, and the old prince gradually does not ask about things and often goes to Xin Zhao to worship Buddha. Xin Zhao is the grand temple of Etok Banner. The halls and meditation rooms are all Chinese-style buildings and are magnificent. The main hall has three floors, with two bronze-clad gold Buddha statues in the middle, each about ten feet high. The Zhao has been built for hundreds of years. More than ten years ago, it was renovated once, costing more than 30,000 taels of silver. There are often hundreds of lamas chanting sutras.

After bidding farewell to the Mongolian officials, we walked along the stream. The clear grass on both sides was like a carpet, and there were countless small flowers, competing for beauty, but I didn't know their names. Suddenly, I saw twenty or thirty strange sheep, with yellow and red hair, long necks, and thin legs, slightly like deer. They were bowing their heads to eat grass. Hearing the sound of footsteps, they suddenly turned their heads to face us. Their horns were sharp and their eyes were bright, as if they were very fierce. I retreated a few steps, but they still raised their heads and did not move. I threw a stone at them, and they fled in a commotion, leaping like flying, reaching a distance of a mile in an instant, and then stood up in a group and looked up as before. I ran back to tell the camel driver. According to the talk, "This is called a yellow sheep, also known as a wild sheep. Since there are many, there must be young ones. Why don't you hunt them quickly?" So we took iron shovels and wooden tools and ran to the original place. The flock of sheep was no longer to be seen, but there were countless hoof prints, deeply embedded in the sand. The land in Inner Mongolia is vast and sparsely populated, with deep artemisia and abundant grass. Yellow sheep breed there, in groups of thousands, with agile spirits. What does a hunter admire? To live and thrive, it can be said that they are self-sufficient.

During this long march of more than ten days, I did not see a single tree. There are no grasslands or forests at all. I heard that near the Yellow River bank, there are abundant red willows, with thin branches growing in clusters, reaching a height of more than ten feet. All the lattice strips used for yurts, as well as the weaving of baskets and sheepfolds, are taken from the red willows. Unfortunately, I have not seen them. In addition, what often catches the eye in the mountains and fields are mostly: 1) Pheasant grass, growing in clusters, six or seven feet high, with tough stems that can be made into ropes. Many pheasants are produced in the grass, which may be the reason for its name. Livestock can eat it. 2) Sophora alopecuroides, the roots have a bitter taste and are a good medicine for throat diseases, that is, mountain soybean roots. The leaves are like sophora, so it is commonly known by that name. 3) Mountain artemisia, green in summer and autumn, yellow in winter and spring. Most of it is mountain artemisia, which camels like to eat. 4) Wolfberry, also a medicine, mostly growing in clusters, with branches three or four feet long. 5) Licorice, shaped like sophora alopecuroides, creeping all over the ground, which can be distinguished after careful observation. 6) Wild wheat, shaped like wheat, with thin leaves and small ears, is the best pasture grass. There is also the so-called "milk grass," which is extremely nutritious for livestock to eat. A Japanese doctor wanted to study this grass and made a trip to Mongolia. No one recognized it, so it was a pity that it could not be identified. 7) Bracteantha bracteata, also growing in clusters, less than a foot high, shaped like a puffball. 8) Cistanche deserticola, shaped like a fish, without branches or leaves showing on the outside, rising from loose soil, which can be dug out. 9) Cynomorium songaricum has a sweet taste and is shaped like a small red radish, used to strengthen yang, but the output is far less abundant than licorice and phellodendron. On the 6th, it was cloudy and not raining in the morning, with strong winds blowing, and the cold was pressing. The grassland was flat and wide, with nothing to block it. The wind came and went without obstruction, so it was more violent than in the inland. In the afternoon, the wind stopped and the clouds cleared. We packed our bags and set off. We first met three Mongolians, with red hats and yellow horses, galloping past quickly. The Baishui River, thirty miles away, was shallow and wide. We crossed the river slowly on the sandy beach, which was soft and undulating, like a spring cushion, which was very interesting. However, the camel's hooves sank deeply with a bang, and white pulp sprayed high, startling the riders and soiling their clothes. There were sand dunes nearby, and the wind blew the sand like a waterfall, which was very beautiful. We stayed overnight at "Ulan Shu," a total of seventy miles. There was a single tree, standing majestically on a high hill, like an umbrella, with broad needle leaves, which could not be seen from afar. The place was named after it. The well water was drinkable.

We set off in the afternoon of the 7th and passed "Ulan Tanzi." In that place, the artemisia grass was burned by fire, and the soil was thousands of acres, with no one asking for farming. Twenty miles away, there were two wells, six feet deep. From here, the Helan Mountains, 300 miles away, a line of blue, were vaguely visible. It is commonly said, "Seeing the mountain is like seeing Ningxia." We couldn't help but feel joyful. Forty-five miles away, we camped at "Kushui Jingzi." That day, we traveled a total of 65 miles. The well was deep and the water tasted bitter, but it was barely drinkable. On the way, there were also Moshui and Fan Shui. The water tasted astringent and bitter. If we had mistakenly stayed at those two stations, not only would it be difficult for people to drink, but even camels would not be able to drink. We had already passed them, which was very fortunate.

Guangdong Province Promotes the Unified Control Policy: The Government Will Manipulate the Economy and Finance: The Salt and Sugar Industries Will Be Monopoly by the Government 88

Shantou Communication: The three-year governance plan advertised by Guangdong Province has a strict promotion of new unified control in its course, such as the economy, finance, agriculture, salt affairs, sugar industry, and industry, etc., which are implemented by the competent authorities and political research associations. For example, the Chaoshan sugar industry has established public warehouses for unified control and implemented government monopoly. Also, recently, various imported goods will be subject to additional taxes. The industrial unified control policy is as follows: 1) Establish an Industrial Improvement Committee to be responsible for handling the unified control affairs of the province. 2) The scope of unified control is limited to factories and industries, and household industries and handicrafts are not included in the unified control. 3) The first phase of the trial is limited to four types: matches, flashlights, rubber, and domestic kerosene. After success, the silk industry and other industries will be promoted. 4) After the implementation of unified control, on the one hand, the tax rate on imported goods will be increased, and the establishment of new factories will be restricted. 5) All factories under unified control, their production volume and output prices, are temporarily approved by the competent authorities, and cannot compete in production and sales. The management, manufacturing, product sales, and transportation of each factory are subject to the supervision and direction of the competent authorities. For example, the second trunk line of the East District Private Highway, Jiahui Road, has now been taken back by the government for traffic, and each section of the highway is supervised and directed by the Highway Bureau. For example, unified control of finance, the Department of Finance promulgated the Silver Market Trading Business Rules, and appointed supervisors to enter the market to supervise trading. It also promulgated the Measures for Silver Industry to Obtain Currency Certificates, Securities Trading, and Copper Yuan Price List to prevent merchants from manipulating finance. On the positive side, in order to reform the currency system, Guangzhou transactions are based on Hao Yang, but for purchasing goods and remittances to other ports, Da Yang must be used. In order to facilitate conversion, merchants often use the purchase and sale of Hong Kong paper as the standard for converting Da Yang. The financial hub of Guangzhou has been manipulated by Hong Kong dollars. The provincial government is now studying the method of changing to the Da Yang standard. Shantou has long used Da Yang as the standard. At the same time, it has adopted the virtual gold standard. Merchants can guarantee the use of a kind of banknote with real estate in the city, called guaranteed banknotes. This banknote has recently shaken its credit due to the decline in the price of guaranteed industries. The Department of Finance took the opportunity to implement a unified control policy and promulgated the Measures for the Issuance of Merchant Warehouse Certificates, allowing Shantou merchants to issue 10 million yuan to rescue finance. However, after the issuance, all the previously circulating guaranteed banknotes, white votes, auxiliary currency certificates, and circulation certificates, etc., must be recovered in stages. At present, the amount of merchant warehouse certificates registered and received in the city has reached 6 million yuan. If the existing guaranteed banknotes, etc., are to be recovered (about 4 million yuan), the actual revenue of the business field is very small. There is a great difference between merchant warehouse certificates and guaranteed banknotes: 1) They are government credit and belong to limited unified control. Each certificate has a face value of more than 100 yuan. Merchant transactions and trade are very convenient, but the market circulation is too large and not suitable for change. 1) They are private credit, and each certificate has a face value of 1 yuan, 5 yuan, 10 yuan, 25 yuan, and 50 yuan. The market treats them the same as cash. Shantou merchant warehouse certificates can be issued this month. Some people predict that these certificates cannot circulate in the same way as cash, and the future is not optimistic. However, after the government actively implements unified control, the provincial bank's banknotes will definitely guarantee the circulation of banknotes in the market and grasp the highest authority in the Chaoshan financial sector. The government's method of unified control of finance is progressing quite smoothly, such as Shantou's repeated prohibition of exporting foreign currency, and each person cannot exceed 20 yuan. In this way, the circulation of finance must be facilitated by remittance. It is heard that the government's strategy to stabilize exchange rates is to set up a remittance management office. All foreign currency (Da Yang) prohibited from export in this province, who need foreign currency or foreign exchange, should go to the office for exchange and issuance. At the same time, the circulation of foreign currency is prohibited in the province. If there are any concealments, they will be punished for disrupting financial crimes. If financial unified control can be successful, then economic unified control will be carried out, and the restriction of consumption in the province and the restriction of the import of foreign goods will be implemented. The restriction method is to increase a kind of protection additional tax and a special patent tax for foreign goods that are suspected of competing with local goods in this province. 1) Increase the additional tax on foreign goods, and the names of the goods have been announced, such as the collection of the Shimin soil additional tax. As for kerosene, paint, and foreign rice, special taxes have been held, and they have been implemented. It is heard that the match and paper cigarette special tax or special operation will follow. It is expected that after the implementation of the economic unified control policy, the financial aspects can increase a large amount of revenue, so it has been decided to start the economic unified control in the second half of the year. There are also agricultural unified control, such as the foreign rice tax that was opened last year, which is the precursor to agricultural unified control. Recently, the sugar industry is being unified, stipulating that the government makes sugar, farmers plant sugar cane, and merchants transport and sell it, almost completely imitating salt affairs. Ten major sugar merchants are selected in the province as operating merchants, and twelve major sugar markets are designated in the province. All sugar transportation should obtain a sugar transportation certificate, otherwise it will be regarded as private sugar. Shantou is one of the largest sugar markets and also a production area of local sugar. Fang Ruilin has been appointed as the director of the sugar warehouse, and many technicians have been sent to measure the establishment of a sugar factory in Jieyang. At present, Chaoshan merchants have stopped transporting sugar for import. Guangzhou is using ships to transport 2,000 packages to Shantou for the market. All those previously operated by merchants are sealed. After that, merchants are not allowed to sell sugar without a license. Even if the people have their sugar cane, they cannot privately own their sugar. (June 20th)

Bandit Gangs Retreat from Huichang; Bandits on the West Road Suddenly Become Rampant; Xiang Army Deploys Defenses in Zixing and Chenzhou 89

Guangzhou Correspondence: Recently, the various armies suppressing the bandits in Jiangxi Province have been pressing closer to the bandit areas, launching a large-scale encirclement that is expected to be completed soon. Representatives from various armies are also gathering in Guangzhou to discuss the overall encirclement plan. As a result, the communist bandits in Jiangxi have also taken clandestine actions, planning to split into two routes to flee horizontally. Currently, a large force from Huichang has been secretly gathering in areas such as Changting and Shicheng. According to news from the front lines, Hu Yanguang, director of the refugee group under the Seventh Division of Huang Yanzhen stationed in Junmenling, reported that refugees fleeing from Mazhou stated: 1. There are no bandits within the city of Huichang. On the Dong side of the river, there are about 2,000 bandits from the pseudo-Newly Organized Third Army Corps and the Protection Section, with about 1,000 rifles. They lack bullets and place four water-cooled machine guns on the Dong River bridgehead every night to guard the city and prohibit people from passing through. 2. The pseudo-Guangdong-Jiangxi Provincial staff has moved to Shangbanling, ten miles east of the city, the Protection Section personnel have moved to Wazipai, twenty-five miles east of the city, and the pseudo-County Soviet has moved to Pengjingcheng, five miles east of the city, and Gaodi, twenty-one miles away. Tilong has four bandit forts and patrol posts. 3. There are only twenty to thirty pseudo-district Soviets in Macheng. 4. There are over three hundred armed bandits from the pseudo-Twenty-second Division in Zhantang, and over a hundred in Nankeng. 5. There are over a hundred bandits from the pseudo-Independent Battalion and the Supply Department in Shangbu and Youshui. 6. The bandits in Huichang are carrying out large-scale massacres, with as many as twenty to thirty people killed every day. It is investigated that the reason why the Huichang bandits retreated so quickly is that since Junmen was captured by the South Road Army, it has lost its stronghold, which it relied on as a barrier to Huichang. Repeated counterattacks only resulted in sacrifices. Since Junmen cannot be recaptured, Huichang can be taken at any time. Therefore, they carried out the deceptive plan of an empty city, first massacring the wealthy in Huichang, causing them to lose their courage and flee, and then forcing the able-bodied men to follow them, ensuring that the city was devoid of wealth and food to trap those who came later. Secondly, they gathered the remaining bandit soldiers from Huichang in one place to act at the right opportunity and preserve the strength of the bandit forces to embark on new routes. It is rumored that the destination of the bandits is western Jiangxi and eastern Hunan. Therefore, the bandits lying in ambush in western Jiangxi are becoming increasingly rampant. The gangs in Lianhua, Yongxin, Suichuan, and Ninggang are planning to unite with the remnants of Li Mingrui's forces in southeastern Hunan. He Jian, the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression army on the west road, has transferred the two divisions of Liu Jianxu and Peng Weiren/Chen Guangzhong to Zixing and Chenzhou in southeastern Hunan to deploy defenses. At the same time, he has also requested Yu Hanmou, the commander of the First Column of the South Road Bandit Suppression Army, to send additional troops to prevent and block the bandits in western Jiangxi. Yu has recently ordered Kong Kequan's Tenth Regiment of the Fourth Division stationed in Shangyou and Chongyi to strictly block and suppress the bandits. He has also ordered the Independent Third Division to send teams to reinforce defense in Lechang and Renhua to strengthen the defense of northern Guangdong. The General Headquarters of the South Road Army also believes that the construction of a blockade line in the bandit areas between Hunan and Guangdong is urgent. Yesterday, it dispatched a delegation of staff members and technical experts led by Director Fan Zongchi to northern Guangdong, including Shaoguan, Nanxiong, Shixing, Lechang, and Pingshi, to inspect the completed fortresses and plan the defense works within the blockade line. (21st)

Establishment of Bandit Suppression Headquarters in the Jiangxi-Anhui Border Area; Appointment of Liao Shiqiao and Others as Commanders 90

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang believes that the bandit atmosphere in this province has gradually subsided, but in the northeastern counties of Jiangxi, there are still remnants of bandits harassing from time to time. It is imperative to eliminate them within a limited time. He has specially established the Jiangxi-Anhui Border Area Bandit Suppression Headquarters, appointing Liao Shiqiao, Director of the Provincial Security Department of this province, as Commander, and Li Leifu, Advisor to the Military Affairs Commission, as Deputy Commander. All staff members are transferred from the three departments of the Executive Headquarters, the Provincial Security Department, and the Qingxiang Aftermath Inspection Group, without additional salaries, to save public funds. After receiving the order, Liao and Li immediately began to organize the establishment, which is now ready. It is also heard that they are scheduled to depart separately today and tomorrow. All affairs of the Security Department are handled by Deputy Director Lai. The areas, tasks, powers, and organization of the headquarters are recorded below: (A) Area: Pengze, Fuliang, Poyang, Hukou, Leping in Jiangxi; Dongliu, Qiupu, Qimen, Wuyuan in northern Anhui. (B) Tasks: 1. Suppress bandits; 2. Supervise the construction of blockhouses and roads; 3. Organize and train the masses, and other local self-defense and aftermath matters. (C) Powers: 1. The commander and deputy commander are both under the command of Commander-in-Chief Chen; 2. The troops and teams stationed in the area are under their command for bandit suppression; 3. The administrative commissioners in the area are under their guidance for pacification; 4. The county magistrates in the area are under their command for pacification; 5. Omitted; 6. The deputy commander may, in accordance with the commander's intentions, directly handle political matters when necessary. (D) Organization: The commander and deputy commander may each set up several staff officers, adjutants, and secretaries, who are all transferred from the staff of the Nanchang Executive Headquarters, the Security Department, and the Qingxiang Aftermath Affairs Inspection Group. No salaries will be paid, but allowances may be granted, and assistants may be appointed to assist. (E) Funding: A temporary fee of 10,000 yuan will be issued in advance, and actual expenses will be reported and reimbursed. (Datong News Agency)

Ministry of Communications Unifies Accounting Administration; Establishes Accounting Director's Office; Hires Experts for Public Audits; Formulates Telecommunications Accounting System; New System Implementation Shows Results 91

Beijing News: Since taking office, Minister of Communications Zhu Jiahua, in order to realize independent accounting, first established the Accounting Director's Office of the Ministry, actively promoting accounting administration. In order to fully understand the current status of the Ministry's accounting administration and its effectiveness, the reporter specifically visited the responsible personnel of the Ministry of Communications yesterday, who gave the following statement: "The postal, telecommunications, and shipping industries under the jurisdiction of the Ministry are mostly public utilities. In recent years, due to national troubles and general economic decline, the transportation industry has been affected, resulting in its economic situation being extremely difficult. However, the imperfect accounting administration and system of the industry itself, the lack of strict auditing of budgets and final accounts, and the lax supervision of business revenues and expenditures are also important reasons. Therefore, after Minister Zhu took office, he first established the Accounting Director's Office of the Ministry to unify accounting administration and make it independent and in a transcendent position. He also hired accounting experts to study and plan with the responsible personnel of the Ministry and formulated a telecommunications accounting system for the subordinate telecommunications agencies to follow. The new accounting initiatives of the Ministry can be reported to you in the following three points: 1. Personnel Improvement: The Ministry, in view of the fact that accounting personnel in the past subordinate agencies have always advanced or retreated according to their superiors and lacked independence, therefore made accounting independent and raised the accounting authority. Special accounting directors, accountants, and cashiers are set up in the subordinate agencies according to the complexity of the affairs to organize offices. All accounting affairs of the agencies are handled by the accounting directors or accountants, and rules for accounting and cashier personnel are formulated for compliance. At the same time, the Ministry feels that there is a shortage of accounting talents and, in order to promote the examination system, in April of this year, it requested the Examination Yuan to hold a temporary examination for accounting

Page 11

personnel to select talents to take charge of sorting out accounting affairs. The successful candidates have now been assigned and employed. In addition, the Ministry feels that the accounting situation of the subordinate agencies has not been strictly audited in the past. Therefore, the Accounting Director's Office has been ordered to set up auditors to go to various places to audit accounts, and inspectors are sent to inspect at any time. On one hand, accountant Pan Xulun is commissioned to go to the subordinate agencies to audit accounts on a regular basis. In addition, accountant Ke Zuoshi is commissioned to send foreign accounting experts to be stationed in important agencies, such as the Postal Administration, the Savings and Remittances Administration, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the International Telecommunications Bureau, the China National Aviation Corporation, and the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, to audit everything in order to be strict and to use this as the basis for sorting out and finding ways to improve efficiency. Although this method is an innovation, it is to seek openness in everything, to show public trust, and to improve the accounting administration and popularize the accounting system. 2. System Innovation: The Ministry, in view of the complex telecommunications business, assets and liabilities, and business profits and losses, must have accurate statistics. Therefore, it convened personnel with accounting knowledge and experience to study and formulate the telecommunications accounting system, such as accounting subjects, accounting regulations, general accounting compilation methods, bookkeeping organization form formats, bookkeeping rules, allocation methods, and procedures for stipulating telecommunications budget, final account, revenue and expenditure, and audit standards. The new system has been ordered to be strictly followed by the subordinate telecommunications agencies and has formulated guidelines for implementing the new system for compliance. In addition, special registration examples are compiled for reference. In addition, in order to strictly control the budget of the subordinate agencies, the agencies are ordered to carefully compile the budget and strictly implement it, so that the budget is worthy of its name and saves public funds. 3.

Effectiveness of Implementation: The above-mentioned two points that have been implemented have been quite effective. For example, in the postal sector, the economy has been declining in recent years. Until the year before last, the loss was more than 10 million yuan. In the 22nd year, it is expected that revenue and expenditure will be offset, or even a surplus. After tightening, the Savings and Remittances Bureau has also become increasingly consolidated and has gained social credit. In more than a year, savings have increased by more than 50%. Now, due to the difficulty of investment, in order to ensure the interests and safety of depositors, many areas have stopped accepting deposits. In terms of civil aviation, the economic situation of China National Aviation Corporation and Eurasia Aviation Corporation was on the verge of bankruptcy the year before last. After the reorganization, China National Aviation Corporation has recently been able to be self-sufficient and has a surplus. Although the Shanghai-Xinjiang line has not been restored in Eurasia Aviation Corporation, internal affairs have also been improved. This phenomenon is creating a new record in the civil aviation industry. In general, the aviation industry in various countries relies on state subsidies to maintain, while China National Aviation Corporation is able to be independent and self-sufficient first. If the Shanghai-Xinjiang line of Eurasia Aviation Corporation can be restored, it is estimated that it can also have a surplus. In terms of navigation administration, after the registration office was abolished, expenses were greatly reduced. In the past, the various navigation bureaus and offices failed to follow the budget for expenditure, but after strict rectification, they are now fully following the budget, the accounts are clear, and the revenue and expenditure are verified. Although the old debts of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company have not been cleared immediately, internal affairs have been improved and the business has become more developed. The business revenue itself has increased by more than one million yuan compared to the past. Speaking only of the shipping industry, there is already a surplus. The Bureau has tightened its efforts and saved a lot of expenses. In terms of telecommunications, there has been obvious progress since the rectification, especially the development and expansion of international telecommunications business is gratifying. With the construction of wired electricity, there is no major expenditure on labor and materials due to the long-term lack of repair of various lines, and with the relationship between old debts and arrears, it can already have a surplus every year. Now, starting from the 23rd year, the new accounting system will be implemented, with the Savings and Remittances Administration as the agent treasury, unifying revenue and expenditure, stabilizing the lives of employees, and it is expected to have more satisfactory results. In order to implement a good accounting system, the Ministry will continue to study the improvement of the accounting administration of the subordinate agencies in the hope that the economy of the transportation industry will become increasingly safe and self-sufficient, and that large-scale construction can be planned and advanced."

Jiangxi Provincial Government Dredges Poyang Lake; Shallow Lakebed Often Causes Disasters; Dredging Will Also Benefit Navigation 92

Raozhou Correspondence: Poyang Lake is close to the Yangtze River and is the general place where the rivers of Jiangxi Province converge. The lake area spans more than three hundred miles. The counties along the lake have fertile land and abundant products. The native products and merchandise of Fu, Xin, Rao, Yuan, and Rui Rivers enter and exit through this route, which is an important route in Jiangxi Province. Recently, due to lack of dredging for many years, the lakebed has been silted up, and the water storage capacity has been decreasing day by day. Whenever mountain floods break out in spring and summer, the upstream rivers pour down, and the river water flows back into the lake, causing widespread flooding and often causing disasters. Although levees have been built along the lake, they are difficult to maintain due to the violent water势, and the farmland along the lake is often flooded. In winter, the lake dries up and navigation becomes difficult. Now, in order to fundamentally prevent floods and facilitate transportation, the Provincial Government has ordered the Water Conservancy Bureau to implement dredging as soon as possible to fully accommodate the amount of water flowing in and avoid flooding. The Bureau Director Yan Tian has gone to various places along the lake to inspect in detail and will immediately start dredging. (June 21)

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance Improves Farmland Tax Collection; Abolishes Original Labor Tax Items and Renames Them Land Value Tax; Trial Implementation in Zhenjiang and Eight Other Counties Starting Next Year 93

Zhenjiang News: In order to sort out the farmland tax of various counties and improve the collection system, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance has specially formulated the following regulations: 1. Draft Regulations for the Collection of Land Value Tax in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province; 2. Measures for Unified Conversion of Tax Rates in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province; 3. Regulations for the Collection of Farmland Tax in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province; 4. Measures for Handling Serial Tickets in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province. Starting from the 23rd year, the original items such as busy silver, grain, reed, and miscellaneous office under the farmland tax of various counties will be abolished and collectively referred to as land value tax. All owners should pay the tax silver in accordance with the provisions of the regulations, and the regulations stipulate the collection date, payment procedures, and penalties for late payment. The draft was once seen in newspapers, but it was the initial draft. It was revised considerably during the eight-county magistrate talk, and then printed and distributed to various sections for opinions. It has been revised no less than three or four times. Until recently, it was roughly revised. The following is an excerpt of the revised draft regulations (according to the draft is for the trial of the improvement of farmland tax in Zhen, Xuan, Li, Cheng, Kun, Jia, Ru, eight counties, after the eight counties have achieved success, it will be formally submitted to the Provincial Government and transferred to the Ministry of Finance for approval).

"Draft Regulations for the Collection of Land Value Tax in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province" 94

Chapter 1, General Provisions: Article 1. The Bureau has specially formulated these regulations in order to sort out the farmland tax of various counties and improve the collection system. Article 2. The original items such as busy silver, grain, reed, and miscellaneous office under the farmland tax of various counties should be abolished from the 23rd year and collectively referred to as land value tax. Article 3. All types of civilian, garrison, reed, and beach farmland within the province, whether public or private, should be paid by the owners in accordance with the provisions of these regulations. Chapter 2

Grading and Tax Rate Article 4. The grades of farmland in each county are divided according to the total amount of old silver and rice regular tax and attached donations per mu, and are divided into grades, limited to three grades and nine grades. Article 5. The land value tax of each county should be collected separately according to the grades, and the tax rate to be collected should be drafted by each county according to its original tax amount and submitted to the Bureau for approval. Article 6. The above two articles regarding the grading of farmland and the rate of tax to be collected in each county shall be handled in accordance with the separately formulated unified conversion method of the land value tax rate. Chapter 3

Collection Date Article 7. The land value tax of each county shall be collected in two phases each year, the first and the second, and each phase shall be paid in one lump sum within two months from the date of collection. The collection date is temporarily divided into the following three types: A. June 1 for the first phase, and October 1 for the second phase; B. July 1 for the first phase, and November 1 for the second phase; C. August 1 for the first phase, and December 1 for the second phase. The application of the above-mentioned collection period by each county shall be stipulated by the Bureau and issued in a list. If there is a necessary situation and the collection period needs to be advanced or extended, the county may state the reasons and submit them to the Bureau for approval, but the end of the second phase of collection shall be limited to the lunar New Year. Article 8. The amount of land value tax collected by each county shall be calculated according to the amount to be collected. The first phase shall collect 40% and the second phase shall collect 60%. The amount of tax reduction to be verified in the autumn survey shall be deducted from the amount of tax in the second phase and shall not be carried over to the next year. Article 9. After the expiration of the two-month collection period for each phase of land value tax, it shall be the collection period. All unpaid households shall be urged to pay by the county government by dispatching police officers. Chapter 4

Payment Procedures Article 10. The land value tax collected by each county shall be collected by the general counter set up by the county government, and branch counters may be set up in the four townships to entrust the county treasury of each county to handle tax collection and remittance. Article 11. The land value tax of each county shall be collected. After the abolition of silver and rice and the unification of the tax rate, the Bureau shall stipulate the new serial form and issue it to each county for printing and use. The handling method of the serial tickets shall be separately stipulated. Article 12. After receiving the land form or notice issued by the county government before the start of the collection period, each owner shall pay the tax price to the general counter or each counter on time and collect the receipt at any time. Article 13. The amount of land value tax collected by each county should be marked in detail on the notice of the provincial and county tax rates, and the wooden signs should be erected at the door of the general and branch counters, and the above-mentioned matters that must be notified should be explained in detail so that the people can watch. If there are still those who do not understand the tax rate, they can go to

The inquiry office inquires at any time. Article 14. The collection of land value tax in each county shall be completed within one month after the expiration of the collection period of each phase, and the tax money for the whole year shall be cleared at the end of each accounting year. It is not allowed to set up year by year. Chapter 5

Penalties for Late Payment Article 15. Those who have not paid the grain within the payment deadline stipulated in Article 7 of these regulations shall be fined separately. The rules for the late payment fine shall be revised separately. Article 16. If the tax due for each phase has not been paid after the expiration of the collection period, in addition to the late payment fine, the case may be filed for arrest and prosecution, and the property may be sealed up for collateral if necessary. Chapter 6

Supplementary Provisions Article 17. Matters concerning the exemption and deferment of land value tax in disaster-stricken years shall be handled in accordance with the regulations promulgated by the Ministry, and with reference to the special circumstances of this province, separate methods shall be formulated. Article 18. Starting from the 23rd year, each county shall handle the autumn survey in advance, no later than the end of August. Article 19. If the owner's real estate is divided or transferred, the grain should be transferred immediately. The rules for grain transfer shall be stipulated separately. Article 20. From the date of implementation of these regulations, all the original silver and rice regular tax, provincial and county surcharges, and various mu donations shall be abolished and changed to provincial tax and county tax. No additional taxes and donations shall be levied in the future. The original mu donations that have expired shall also be stopped collecting on time. Article 21. The rules for the collection of land value tax in each county shall be formulated separately. Article 22. The detailed rules for the implementation of these regulations shall be drafted by each county with reference to the county's situation and submitted to the Department of Finance for approval. Article 23. These regulations shall be implemented after deliberation and promulgation by the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee. (25th)

The Second Day of the Agricultural Warehouse Meeting in Various Counties; It Was Resolved That the Warehouse Location and the Agent Organization Be Merged; Storage, Mortgage, Transportation, and Sales Shall Be Handled by the County Warehouse Committee 95

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The details of the first day of the agricultural warehouse meeting of 29 counties convened by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday (26th), the group discussions were held, with each three counties as a group, and each group discussed for 30 to 50 minutes. The discussion started at 8 am and ended at 6 pm. Due to the different environments of each county, the resolutions were very complicated. To summarize the main points, they are roughly as follows: 1. Determine the location of the warehouses in each county, and the original agent organizations shall be merged and handled uniformly. 2. Decide on the methods of purchase, storage, and mortgage, with storage and mortgage as the main focus, and transportation and sales shall be handled by the County Agricultural Warehouse Committee, and loans shall be made by the bank. 3. Processing equipment shall be determined specifically according to the situation of each county. 4. Regarding transportation and sales, the Agricultural Warehouse Management Committee shall contact the Shanghai Agricultural Products Transportation and Sales Office separately. Also, it is reported that the Department of Finance believes that the gradual promotion of agricultural warehouses in various counties involves a lot of affairs. If there is no special management organization, it is very inconvenient for the progress of the business. Therefore, it is necessary to actively organize the Provincial Agricultural Warehouse Management Committee. It is heard that the planning has started and will be realized soon. (27th)

Songjiang; Public Security Bureau Merges Sub-Stations 96

The County Public Security Bureau previously received an order from the Provincial Government, roughly to the effect that it should reorganize the establishment to save police expenses and focus on police capacity to increase efficiency, and should report the plan for implementation in July. The autonomous region of this county has now been merged into eight districts, and the police districts should be re-determined. A police affairs meeting was convened on the 27th, presided over by Director Zhou Ding, and all the heads of the sub-bureaus and all the inspectors attended. Many case precedents were discussed. Regarding the issue of merging sub-stations, in accordance with the methods promulgated by the province, it was decided that the four sub-stations in the urban and suburban areas should be preserved, and the six sub-stations in Wu Ku, Xiao Kun, Qi Bao, Zhang Ze, Chen Jiahang, and Xinqiao should be abolished. The remaining police were incorporated into nearby bureaus. After the resolution was made, it was submitted in writing.

A Large Gambling Den Yields Nothing 97

Gambling is rampant in this county. Although the public security organs have repeatedly investigated and detained those who violate the law, there are still those who dare to violate the prohibition to collect head taxes and gather for gambling. Today (27th) afternoon, the Public Security Bureau received a report that a certain Zhang had opened a stall on the north side of Baojia Bridge outside the west gate, where the wins and losses were very large every day, and there was public no fear. The inspector Zhu was dispatched to lead the special team to ambush and arrest them. However, the gambling house had a lookout. Seeing that the police were approaching, they had packed up and cleaned up, and the gamblers were all slipped away. Such meticulousness shows the scale of the operation.

Suzhou; Suzhou Has Been Very Hot for Days 98

Suzhou has been very hot until yesterday (27th), which was the third day. The humidity was steamy, and it was not cool all night. At about 5 pm on the 26th, the temperature in ordinary places reached 102 degrees. Yesterday afternoon at 1 pm, the indoor temperature was also as high as 100 degrees. For days, residents have been sleeping in the streets of the city at night, like snails out of their shells. Fans in all electrical appliance stores in the city have been sold out.

The former Wu County Public Security Bureau Chief Shen Gao Chen was ordered to be transferred to Changshu County Public Security Bureau Chief. After Shen handed over the tasks of Wu County, he originally intended to go to Changshu to take over the job. He has already submitted his resignation to the Department of Civil Affairs.

Wuxi: Bizarre Bloodshed at the Defense Corps 100

In the Second Squad, Second Platoon of the Defense Corps of Shangshan Township, Huaixia City, Eighth District, a bizarre murder occurred on the morning of the 26th. A cook and a soldier of the corps were killed and wounded. The deceased was named Han Zike, a native of Shouxian County, Anhui Province, 30 years old, who had enlisted for three or four years. The injured was named Han Weibiao, 40 years old, a native of Siyang, who worked as a cook in the squad. Usually, the two slept in the same room. Zike had an affair with Yue, the wife of Zhu Genbao of nearby Ni'jia Lane. Recently, their relationship soured. On the afternoon of the 25th, Zhu Yue argued with Zike at the squad headquarters and took away his watch and undershirt. This was learned by squad leader Zhu Meiji, who dismissed Han Zike for his misconduct. Zhu Yue was also scolded by her husband and attempted suicide but was rescued. At 10:30 a.m. on the 26th, a gunshot was suddenly heard in Han's room. Nearby residents went to investigate and found Han Zike dead, lying supine on the bed, a Mauser pistol beside his right hand, a spent cartridge under his crotch, a complete bullet next to his right shoulder, and two gunshot wounds on his chest and below his left breast. Han Weibiao was shot once in the abdomen, pressing his hand to his stomach, and squatting on the ground. Villagers reported to the squad detective Zhu Meiji, who ordered the injured man to be sent to the city and reported the situation to the company commander Gu Weijun, saying that Han Zike had shot and wounded Han Weibiao and then committed suicide. Afterwards, Tan Weinan, the director of the 16th Public Security Bureau in charge, also rushed to the mountain to investigate. They found Zhu Yue locked in the squad headquarters with iron chains. According to Zhu Xiangping, the deputy squad leader, the case was caused by jealousy between Zike and Weibiao. However, another version is that Zike resented Weibiao after being dismissed, so he shot and wounded him before committing suicide. In short, the case is extremely bizarre and complicated, and the content may be more than this simple. The township chief Qin Fengming has reported to the local branch court, requesting an autopsy. The acting prosecutor led officials to the village to conduct the autopsy on the morning of the 27th and confirmed that Han Zike had shot and killed himself. After the autopsy, they returned to the court to await investigation and handling.

Silk Merchants Firmly Oppose Improvement Tax 101

The eighteen silk factories, including Xinyi, in this county, considered the improvement fee levied for the construction of the hall unaffordable. They repeatedly petitioned the model district of this county, requesting the revocation of the order, but were not approved. The manufacturers also sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, asking the county to consider the plight of the silk merchants and exempt them from payment, but so far there has been no solution. The factories had no choice but to file an administrative appeal with the Executive Yuan yesterday. At the same time, they sent another letter to the county chamber of commerce, requesting it to forward the letter to the model district to retain the funds already collected. If the appeal fails, they are willing to pay, otherwise, they must be returned in full, and no deliberate difficulties should be created at that time. After receiving the letter, the county chamber of commerce has forwarded the letter to the model district for verification.

Measures for Handling Opium Pill Cases 102

The anti-smoking committee members Qian Sunqing, Cheng Jingang, and Li Tiping, in view of the county public security bureau's recent searches for opium and red pills in stores and residences, which have caused great disturbance, sent a letter to the county government to express their views. Magistrate Yan, who is also the chairman of the anti-smoking committee, convened a meeting of the anti-smoking committee yesterday and resolved: (1) Issue a notice immediately to encourage people to quit smoking and drugs. (2) The opium pill offenders arrested by the public security bureau in recent days will be dealt with according to the following items: (A) Those who supply people with opium pills for sale and consumption will be sent to the province for interrogation. (B) Those who consume opium pills will be released on bail, with a guarantee of availability upon request, and will be given a deadline of two months to quit. After the deadline, they will be summoned and examined. Those without a guarantor will be temporarily detained and sent to the drug rehabilitation hospital after it is established. (3) Regarding the reporting of opium pill cases, we will petition the provincial government to strictly enforce the measures against false accusations and retaliatory actions.

Changshu: Severe Drought and Strange Heat; Xin Feng Pavilion Destroyed 103

The weather here suddenly became strangely hot starting from the 25th. In addition, since the beginning of summer, there has been no rain, and the fields in various townships have cracked, creating a drought. The villagers are all worried. At 8 p.m. on the 25th, four farmers from the eastern township secretly went up Mount Yu with axes and ropes, and suddenly chopped off the corners of Xin Feng Pavilion. When it collapsed, there was a loud noise. This was heard by the staff of the meteorological station on the mountain, who went out to check and saw the villagers had gone down the mountain and fled. It is said that the severe drought is because there is a lurking dragon under Xin Feng Pavilion, which can be activated to bring rain by chopping it down. Although this is superstitious, the farmers' eagerness for rain is evident here.

Jiangyin: Water Police Seize Illegally Held Military Weapons 104

Xu Shaoqiao, the former captain of the water police, lived in Liuyigang, Jingjiang. After leaving office, he ran a local business and had considerable wealth. He is now the head of the Seventh District Defense Corps in the county. The other day, Jiang Fubao, on patrol boat No. 2 of the Third Squad of the Liuyigang water police, went to Xu Shaoqiao's house and seized more than 400 rounds of quick-firing rifle bullets and 160 Mauser pistol rounds. He immediately reported to He Zhiping, the captain of the Third Squad. Because He was a sworn brother of Xu, he delayed reporting it. On the 24th, Jiang Fubao believed that Xu's illegal possession of military weapons was a major case, so he crossed the river to Yin and reported to Captain Huang. Captain Huang dispatched patrol officer Jin Jishan and others to Liuyigang to seize the guns and bullets and take them back to the squad headquarters, pending investigation and reporting to the district headquarters for verification and handling.

The Jiangyin County Government, in handling the land dispute case of Yu Chunfa, discovered that Chen Shouting, a dismissed clerk of the county government, was falsely using the name of the county government to survey land in the countryside, secretly helping Huang Quanfu, Sun Linsheng, and others to destroy boundary markers and establish new boundaries, committing the crimes of swindling and deceiving.
